               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2015-06-01" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   6/1/2015
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Koiso has all the right decor and affectations of a good traditional Japanese restaurant, and has all the right things on the menu to support this. The actual dining experience, however, was surprisingly mediocre.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Judging by the other reviews maybe my experience was on an off day. The waiters and others running the restaurant seemed stressed out and over-worked, but there were not many people actually at the restaurant other than a pushy and obnoxious family with several small children, which understandably can ruin a waiter's day. It took nearly 15 minutes for someone to take our order, and the food which was simple in nature took forever to come out. Normally I don't care about service if the food was good, however suffice to say it was not.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We ordered the cold tofu appetizer. This was refreshing when dipped into the sort of ginger-soba sauce it came with, but you could see the "recycle" imprint on the bottom of the tofu block that the tofu was just firm tofu from a plastic package that you could just buy at the local grocery.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Then we got the Omakase, which for $35 is a steal, however the sushi was sub par. There was some sort of fluke swimming in some sort of ponzu that suspiciously overwhelmed its flavor. The nigiri had so much wasabi gluing the fish on top that it was equally overwhelming and difficult to eat. The salmon was bland. The octopus was actually quite good, tender and sweet. Overall, though, the sushi was surprisingly tasteless.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The only saving grace here was likely the ramen, though I did not like it as much as my fiance did. I generally prefer Tonkatsu or Shio ramen, and I believe this ramen was of the Shoyu type. The ramen had a good texture, the soup had a big hunk of pork belly in it, and the soup itself was pretty rich and a little briny. The pork belly was not in chashu form, but rather was unseasoned and un-seared. The egg was over cooked and crumbled into the soup. My opinion is that if you want ramen in this area go to Torigo for lunch instead, but as ramen is hard to find in LI, I'd give this one a pass.
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-07-01" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   7/1/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  4.5 starts.
                  <br/>
                  I went there twice. Last winter and last weekend. After I went there for the first time, I was thinking to rate them 4 starts, but I decided to give them more stars after the second visit. I tried to come here few months ago, too, but they were closed because it was Sunday. Please remember that they are closed on Sunday. They have spacious parking lot in the back of the restaurant.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  This is not fancy restaurant, and kind of old, but there is warm feeling like I was at home. I felt like I was visiting someone's family in Japan. It was nostalgic feeling.
                  <br/>
                  I had ramen and gyoza(dumpling) when I ate there for the first time. It was soy sauce soup ramen. It was served with my favorite ingredients, Chasu(sliced roasted pork), pickled bamboo shoot, Nori and boiled egg. It is very authentic ramen. Gyoza was just like my mother's in Japan. My boyfriend ordered ramen at his first visit and he liked it, so he ordered it again.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  When I went there for the second time, I ordered Yamakake Soba ( buckwheat noodle with grated yam.) There are choice of cold or hot, so I chose hot. The noodle was in hot soy sauce soup with has a lot of Umami came from fish. I assume the broth was taken from bonito flakes. Grated yam is white and slimy, and it is supposed to be healthy food. On the soba, they sprinkled shredded nori and put a quail egg in the center. I loved this Yamakake Soba!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Today's special food was very good. We orderede two specials from the menu. The first one was Fried Egg Plant with gingers and green onionsNasu Shigiyaki. The lady who served food explained to us that eggplant was grown in their backyard. Very fresh and flavorful! The second special was Seared Bonito fish (Katsuo no Tataki). It was just like the one I eat my hometown in Japan.
                  <br/>
                  Since my boyfriend doesn't understand Japanese, it was funny that wait staff ladies explain about menu in Japanese sometimes. But it made them look cute for me. I think my boyfriend doesn't care and he seemed enjoying eating there. Actually he is the one who suggested to go back there.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  They don't accept American Express card. I leaned this because they gave us the check on the tray with Amex Logo whihc was crossed out. Haha.
                 </p>

                 <span class="js-expandable-comment comment-truncated">
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable">
                   My family and I have been going to this place since we moved to Carle Place in '07. My Hubby &amp; I
                  </span>
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable hidden">
                   My family and I have been going to this place since we moved to Carle Place in '07. My Hubby &amp; I personally love their Grilled to perfection fish/catch of the day,.so tasty and flavorful, freshest sashimi that melts in your mouth and sushi's to die for! Squid appetizer and spicy tuna, something that you may want to try for yourself. Mitz and Kioko are the most wonderful host that you could ever find, very attentive and nice couple. Place is family and kid friendly!

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-08-27" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   8/27/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I was on the fence about writing a review for this place for a couple of reasons and mostly because it seems like it would not matter that much anyway because Koiso it seems has long time regulars that keep this place running.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Like other reviewers said it seems you may get better service and attention if you are a regular. We popped in later in the evening and directed to a table from the couple behind the sushi bar. We proceeded to wait a good 10 minutes before we even received a menu. It was another 10 minutes after we were ready to order before it was taken. It was another 50 minutes or so before we got our food with the place nearly empty.. see where I am going with this. Be prepared to wait - luckily we were because we weren't starving when we walked in although the wait helped with that.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  During our wait we saw how the sushi chef and the two other women were catering to the regulars - making conversation, serving up omakase at the sushi bar, catching up with regulars that had not been there for a while. It's not to say our service was rude - it was just not overly friendly towards us. Also everyone seemed very busy all the time - it must be said it didn't seem like anyone was slacking just this is the pace they operate.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We ordered some sushi rolls to share and have to say this was some of the best tasting sushi we had on long island. The rolls were a little on the pricy side, but they were also made a bit larger both more fish and rice then most places make their sushi. We were pleasantly surprised at real crab in one of the special rolls we ordered - we noticed the difference immediately from the imitation crab that is prevalent at most places. The yellow tail was some of the best we ever tasted.
                  <br/>
                  You can tell there is a reason this place has a long time following (seems they followed them from their old location in Port Washington, that must have been a while ago because this place looks like it has been open for a while with a lot of wear and tear.).
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Besides the slow service (which was bearable) here's what made our visit so disappointing and why we probably will not return. While a waitress was cleaning a table she took a half empty glass of water that one of the patrons did not finish and spilled it onto the table to wipe it down. This is perhaps one of the grossest things ever witnessed in a restaurant (which I am glad my wife spared telling me about until AFTER dinner). Its like why bother cleaning the table if you are just going to spread someones backwash all over it?
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Like I said.. this review probably doesn't even matter because it seems they have a loyal, long time following. Even with the sushi being some of the best we had in the area there are just some things I can't get past. Its not that I'm unrealistic - I can only imagine what goes on behind the scenes in most restaurants, but to do this out in the open like that - it's an image my wife cant get out of her head (which means I can't get it out of my head either. lol) . If you can get past it you will be treated to some really good sushi, albeit with slow service.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The sushi and food itself gives this place 5 stars. A 1-2 star average for everything else, thus 3 stars.
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_1" title="1.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="1.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="1.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-12-28" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   12/28/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  We must have caught it on an off day, but two friends and I went to this place around 8 on a Saturday night, and it was some of the most off-putting sushi I have ever seen. All the claims about freshness were unwarranted compared to the fish we got, which was clearly soft, mushy, and not fresh considering fibers were tearing from each other and bunched up on the rice to make the piece seem fuller.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The menu seemed to cover the basics, but we got the $24 "Koiso" set, which was vastly overpriced. It included a standard bowl of miso soup, a bowl of salad, and then a dish that contained 6 pieces of nigiri-sushi (2 tuna, 2 salmon, and 2 yellowtail) and your choice of roll (6 pieces of a normal ,maki-sushi). All 6 pieces of nigiri-sushi were ill-colored, soft, and falling apart, with what seemed like randomly-assigned amounts of wasabi on each piece. Some had normal amounts and some seemed like the wasabi had just be globbed on under the fish, making for a very sudden and strange surprise.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Other items on the menu included a $30 chirashi, which is a pricepoint I don't even see in Manhattan, most of the time.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  It was quiet when we went in, with barely 4 tables having customers (remember this was a Saturday night), so we didn't have trouble in flagging down service, but the food really brought our expectations down the pipe, which was surprising considering how many good reviews this place had (which was what inspired us to try it out in the first place). So either the reviews above were from a different era for the restaurant, or we unfortunately caught it on a VERY bad day.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Either way, will not be returning again, and I don't recommend it at all.
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-06-18" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   6/18/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  After living in Japan for 5 years, Koiso is the place I go when I am craving food from my time abroad. I live in the city, but it is conveniently located right behind the Carle Place Long Island Railroad Station so an easy walk from the train. Once you enter, it as if you are transported into a small version of Japan.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Both the restaurant's atmosphere and food are home style. Koiso is owned by a cute couple, husband Mitsu who you can find behind the sushi bar and wife Kyoko who is out on the floor (or behind the counter when things get busy). Their warm welcome will make you feel like you have found a true neighborhood place similar to Cheers.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The food at Koiso is unbelievable. For people who know Japanese food and are looking for the real thing, Mitsu serves up incredibly authentic dishes you won't find on the menu, such as his shio kara (salt preserved squid) and nuka miso tako (octopus). For those looking for more traditional fare, winners are the homemade shumai (shrimp dumplings) and gyoza (pork dumplings), and the crowd pleasing nasu shigi (eggplant with ginger). Mitsu serves only the freshest fish, and some of the sushi I've had at Koiso is better than what I've had in Japan. Try Koiso once and you are sure to become a regular at this place where everyone knows your name!
                 </p>
                 <ul class="photo-box-grid clearfix js-content-expandable">

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Simply AMAZING!! Even though they are always closed on Sundays, and Saturday lunch....( which is a little bit disappointed) a little story here: we went there three times before we finally arrived at a time when it's open. LoL. But it's totally worth it. From smallest appetizer, to bigger noodle soup and sushi roll, everything is so delicious. I recommend Aged Tofu, Eel sushi, Udon and Shumai!

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-16" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/16/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I normally don't venture out to this part of LI to eat sashimi, but my boyfriend's family recently moved to Mineola so we had to find a local authentic Japanese spot to quench our occasional cravings. We found Koiso through the friendly yelp community. We eliminated all the other nearby choices bc we prefer a no frills restaurant - not interested in paying a premium for loungey sushi. We knew Koiso was the right choice when we saw photos of the humble interior and exterior of the restaurant.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We felt the homey vibe as soon as we walked in, and we immediately knew that we were about to indulge in an authentic Japanese dining experience (and we sure did).
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We went with the $35 omakase, which was served with three appetizers:
                  <br/>
                  - ginger scallion eggplant with special house sauce
                  <br/>
                  - fluke soup with ground daikon
                  <br/>
                  - squid in spicy butter sauce with scallions
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Omakase was very fresh and served with various pieces of sashimi and sushi. Go with a group if you want a larger variety.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We interacted with extremely friendly Japanese staff of a sushi chef and two servers.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  There is a private parking lot in the back - you need to enter from the next block (Broadway). We parked in Carvel's lot accidentally but had no trouble.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I didn't see the restaurants hours of operation on yelp, so I took a pic of it at the restaurant (see attached). Please note that Koiso is closed on Sundays.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-06-08" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   6/8/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  The freshest sushi on Long Island. Delicious, well prepared and presented.
                  <br/>
                  The place is adorable, with traditional Japanese tables. I sat at the sushi bar and let the chef / owner "Mitz" make me a "special plate," and it was delicious. Some of the tastiest sushi ever.
                  <br/>
                  Started with a vegetable tempura. Light, crispy, and the right amount of seasoning.
                  <br/>
                  Its the service of owners Mitz, and his wife Kioko, that make it worth coming back.
                 </p>
                 <ul class="photo-box-grid clearfix js-content-expandable">
                  <li style="width: 348px; height: 348px;">

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-10-26" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   10/26/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  First time here, and it was the freshest sashimi ever. It was caught the same day! I had the ramen as well, and it was very good... Nice springy noodles and tasty homemade broth. I wish there were more types of Ramen soup available but I do understand this is not a "ramen house" per se. I'll be going back to try their rolls and gyoza soon. Pretty sure that I will not be disappointed as I've heard how fantastic they are. The couple are absolutely adorable, treated us as if we're regulars which I believe we will be now. hehe
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Update: Been back a few times, and had their tempura soba noodle soup and jumbo handmade gyoza. I also tried a couple bites of their pork katsu (skewer). All these dishes were fantastic. The pork katsu was tender, not dry like many other restaurants as they use a different cut instead of the usual pork chops.
                 </p>
                </div>

                 <span class="js-expandable-comment comment-truncated">
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable">
                   I travel to long island every couple months and try new restaurants each time and I have to say the
                  </span>
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable hidden">
                   I travel to long island every couple months and try new restaurants each time and I have to say the sushi was absolutely amazing and fresh. The owners husband and wife were absolutely wonderful and as friendly as can be. They have been there for 15 years at this location which says a lot about a restaurant. I got the chefs choice and he put an amazing platter together that was as fresh as can be and he was so proud of his food you could see it when he was talking about it. Take my advice go visit this restaurant if you are in need of a sushi fix and on the island. I will add this restaurant to my must visit each time I am back in Long Island.
                  </span>

                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_1" title="1.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="1.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="1.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2015-01-08" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   1/8/2015
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I went here based on good yelp reviews. We had the garden salad which had a questionable taste, but was ok. Next the vegetable tempura which was actually very good. Last the sushi. The fish tasted way fishy and was cut into small pieces in the rolls like it was the scraps. We had to send back one roll because it was inedible, even when soaked in wasabi and soy sauce. The ginger was floppy, not crisp. And the service was very slow; one waitress for the entire place. Never again.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-09" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/9/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Found this place thru YELP
                  <br/>
                  and the overwhelming positive reviews made me curious.....and overall I would agree with the other ratings and comments
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  My wife and I are avid Sushi lovers and living in NY, we have the opportunity to try the different places. So I kinda have some experience in this cuisine and dining experience.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  At first, the exterior decor of the place would of lead me to think its some low grade Japanese restaurant....but I was wrong. It appears to be a small, cozy husband and wife business. It was "ok" for "date night" dining experience...this is mainly because a large family of 10 can create significant volume in a 500 sq ft room.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I believe the owners strive for the authentic Japanese experience. Everything looked like it was made "in-house" vs. from a supplier; e.g. menus, chop stick paper wrap, etc. This led me to believe the ginger was pickled by them and the wasabi is freshly made....also requesting "extra"will have additional costs!!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I had salmon, tuna, fatty tuna (blue fin at the time), and yellow tail. All were fresh, I would safely say same day delivery to serve.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Hot sake was pretty refreshing, though this is considered the lower grade sake as compare to cold. There's only one brand of choice for both; beer and wine is only alcohol beverages available.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The only reason I gave it 4 stars vs 5, mainly due to the pricing. There are competitors within 5 miles, that have comparative, in some cases better, sushi with lower cost.
                 </p>
                 <ul class="photo-box-grid clearfix js-content-expandable">
                  <li style="width: 348px; height: 348px;">
                   <div class="photo-box photo-box--interactive">
                    <img alt="Koiso Japanese Restaurant - Carle Place, NY, United States. Squid Appetizer" class="photo-box-img" height="348" src="//s3-media1.fl.yelpcdn.com/bphoto/_cf2nC_70PHH3SnFqqKUlA/348s.jpg" width="348"/>
                    <div class="photo-box-overlay js-overlay">
                     <div class="photo-box-overlay_caption">
                      Squid Appetizer
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <a class="biz-shim js-lightbox-media-link" href="/biz_photos/koiso-japanese-restaurant-carle-place?reviewid=v2RsTiaH5d-iamCqRzaFpw&amp;select=_cf2nC_70PHH3SnFqqKUlA">
                     <span class="offscreen">
                      Squid Appetizer
                     </span>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_1" title="1.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="1.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="1.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-26" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/26/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Sad little place. Bland, warm sushi. Cold, slow, non-attentive service. I still feel nauseous hours after not finishing this lousy meal. Server was nice until regulars came in, then we felt quarantined. Had to beg to get check and pay our bill. You have choices folks, you can do much better in this area.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-09-22" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   9/22/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/my-snobby-sushi-list-new-york-2" title="My top to bottom favorite Japanese restaurants that serve sushi.">
                     My snobby Sushi list
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Yes, I've been on a Omakase kick as of late. So I met a Japanese person a while back and I always like to ask where Japanese people like to eat. So, she named a few places in the city and she said she really loved Koiso in LI. So I bookmarked it and finally trekked to the LI to give it a try, it's in the middle of no where...
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  It's run by a cute husband and wife couple from Japan. They are very nice and very hospitable. They have been doing sushi in LI for about 30 yrs. They used to have a shop in Port Washington, now they have been in their current location for about 13 yrs. So when I get there, I ask the wife who greets me, if I could sit at the bar and she replies, "Unfortunately it's not setup but you could sit at a table." =( So I sit at the table and order gyoza since it's made in house, and while I am looking at the menu, I didn't see anything for Omakase. So when the wife comes to take the rest of my order, I asked her about the Omakase and she says it's $35 and you could sit at the bar. My eyebrow went up lol She quickly apologized and says, that a lot of people aren't aware the sushi bar is for, you guessed it, sushi and people like to sit at the bar and order ramen and cooked items. I immediately told her it was perfectly fine and I proceeded to take my seat at the sushi bar. =) The wife then asks, if I was in a rush and if I wanted all the sushi pieces on one plate or if I had time and have the sushi in sets, as it's meant to be. I decided to go with the latter. The first thing about the sushi that sticks out is the freshness of the fish and the amazing texture of the rice. So the Omakse is 9 pieces for $35 and I order extra pieces because that's how I do. When I ordered my first set of extra sushi, it was fine, when I order the second set, the chef says, "You are not done?" bahahahaaha I told him, if he's going to make to make a good quality product, I will keep ordering. I also got brownie points from the wife when she noticed I was only dipping the fish, she said "Oh, you know that?" I was thinking about saying, "Hey lady, this isn't my first time around the rodeo." lol
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The food:
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Gyoza- the gyoza was nice, it is definitely homemade. The texture of the dough is nice and crisp, the filling was good not great for me. It was slightly under flavored for me and kinda pricey for $8.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Omakase plate 1- fluke, snapper, sea bass, striped bass and octopus nigiri. All the sushi was delicate in flavor and all paired nicely with the subtle sweetness from the rice.
                  <a href="http://www.yelp.com/user_local_photos?select=hhv532edtIqkAMulRLWr0Q&amp;userid=Y_iTTjKvV5hLy-880SZzlA">
                   yelp.com/user_local_phot
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Omakase plate 2: sardine and mackerel nigiri. I never heard of sardine sushi but it was quite good and I normally hate mackerel but the one here is nicely flavored.
                  <a href="http://www.yelp.com/user_local_photos?select=AlMWSwKfi4O-eIZnpCKIBQ&amp;userid=Y_iTTjKvV5hLy-880SZzlA">
                   yelp.com/user_local_phot
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Omakase plate 3: Medium toro and Uni nigiri. I am still not completely in love with toro, it was nice but not amazing. Uni is usually my fav but the one here was just OK. The Uni had a slightly off putting taste to it.
                  <a href="http://www.yelp.com/user_local_photos?select=QdarGJJ-JvM7EB3F2eWrmg&amp;userid=Y_iTTjKvV5hLy-880SZzlA">
                   yelp.com/user_local_phot
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Side order 1- Yellowtail and salmon nigiri. I ordered these because they are usually the best tasting fishes and I really liked both here. The Chef also told me he didn't put these in my Omkase because you could get it any where and he wanted to give me something that he appreciates.
                  <a href="http://www.yelp.com/biz_photos/koiso-japanese-restaurant-carle-place?select=e6K2fBDI3OMiAfqi52ZX5A#e6K2fBDI3OMiAfqi52ZX5A">
                   yelp.com/biz_photos/kois
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Side Order 2- Unagi Nigiri. This is another one of my standbys. I thought the fish was a tad sweet from the sauce but still had great flavor.
                  <a href="http://www.yelp.com/biz_photos/koiso-japanese-restaurant-carle-place?select=e6K2fBDI3OMiAfqi52ZX5A#ssksrSaxBHr4V_au8CumBw">
                   yelp.com/biz_photos/kois
                  </a>
                 </p>
                 <ul class="photo-box-grid clearfix js-content-expandable">
                  <li style="width: 348px; height: 348px;">
                   <div class="photo-box photo-box--interactive">
                    <img alt="Koiso Japanese Restaurant - Carle Place, NY, United States. Side order: Unagi nigri" class="photo-box-img" height="348" src="//s3-media2.fl.yelpcdn.com/bphoto/ssksrSaxBHr4V_au8CumBw/348s.jpg" width="348"/>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-11-06" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   11/6/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Very impressive! Traveled here on business and was craving Japanese food. I didn't feel like staying in, so I took some to go.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The fish was surprisingly fresh. I got a couple of rolls as well as the Ten Don. Everything was nicely packed (for all you takeout folks) and it was all still surprisingly good when I got back to the hotel.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Folks there were extremely helpful and nice. They treated me as if I was staying in while I waited. Tea, salad, etc. the works.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  If I'm ever in the area again, I'm going back!!! :)!!
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-01-01" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   1/1/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   4 check-ins
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  One of my favorite places for sushi in the Long Island area. Great place to stop in for dinner after shopping at the Roosevelt Fields Mall, only 2ish miles away. The owners are really nice. It's a homely mom and pop shop. We stop by when we are in the area. In addition to street parking, they have a lot in the back.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  They don't have too many specials rolls, but they are pretty damn good. They do a great job tightly rolling the sushi so it doesn't come apart. My favorite is the Sunset roll. Never thought sweet potato would jive with rolls. I also really like the special shrimp and hot crunchy rolls. The Alaskan roll, double dragon, and firecracker are ok. I would skip the shumai though. We usually order four rolls when we come here. The last time they were kind enough to split the rolls onto two plates.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-06-07" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   6/7/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   2 check-ins
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Was hoping this place would deliver some authentic japanese food and it did. You see on long island japanese food is either sushi, teriyaki, or hibachi steakhouse. All americanized versions of each. Where are the ramen spots.... or places where you can get cheap yakitori (a la Oh Taisho and Ippudo in manhattan). I saw another fellow yelper suggest Koiso. Its a small mom and pop restaurant in Carle Place. A very very very nice husband and wife runs the place with their son/grandson? It wasn't busy for a sat evening. I gotta say the service here is fantastic. We were told of some specials that they had while we were ordering our appetizers which were good suggestions. It wasn't busy in there so I'm sure a different experience will be had when its packed.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  They have a great menu with both yakitori, ramen and some other items you dont see on most menu's. In regards to the food I want to give everyone a bit of advice. If you have a favorite dish that you do not see on the menu chances are they will make it for you! Look at other yelpers reviews and pictures. I saw someone had ordered chicken katsu curry which is one of my favorite dishes. When I was looking at the menu it wasn't on there but when I asked for it the server said of course we can make that for you. My GF got an assortment of sushi. The sushi was REALLY good. Everything was perfectly made. My curry dish was amazing and it was a huge portion. I definitely want to come back and try some other items on the menu. The prices are a bit up there. I know they have to compete with the larger chain restaurants in the area but I have had similar meals for much less in NYC.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  So as long as you dont mind the price and want to try something really special I would highly suggest you check this place out.
                 </p>
                </div>

                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-07" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/7/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  After our week long trip to Japan, my wife and I were CRAVING authentic japanese restaurant. But everywhere we went (exception for few expansive manhattan locations), the taste and sushi quality werent the same. Then we found this place, very close to our house. WHO KNEW! - (YELP knew...)
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Ramen, unagi, gyoza... all reminded me of Japan and they were all so fresh. Price can feel abit higher but you are paying for its freshness and all the work thats put into the preparation. The husband and wife are two very nice people and we had such a heart-warming lunch.
                 </p>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Very nice place. Very clean. It's valentines day so it's very busy and I felt bad for the only waitress there, she was elderly. Food was very good. Potatoes with the terriyaki combo was a little strange but the beef negamaki was so delicious. The udon was perfect and the rolls were good. Just wish there was another waitress helping out.

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-02-18" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   2/18/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   2 check-ins
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Pretty solid sushi joint. Dined here with my boyfriends immediate family and grandparents on Saturday night. We entered through the rear of the restaurant and were seated right away. It wasn't as busy as I was expecting at 7:30 on a Saturday evening.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  My boyfriend and his family spoke very highly of this establishment, so my expectations going in were very high, and I am sad to say, it just did not fully live up to it.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Everyone ordered their own things, while my boyfriend and I decided to order 5 different rolls to split between the two of us. I ordered a shrimp tempura roll and a spicy tuna roll. He ordered an eel avocado roll, sunset roll, and special mushroom roll. I also ordered shumai. The shumai were the first to arrive. They were average at best. The dipping sauce was tasteless and they weren't very hot. As for the rolls, some were far better than others. The most offensive thing was the shrimp tempura roll. At most places, avocado and cucumber are added to this. Instead I just got this sad looking roll with small pieces of chewy shrimp and undercooked tempura batter. No sauce or anything dressing it either. Such a bummer. The spicy tuna roll was pretty good. What my boyfriend ordered was much better than my two sad rolls! The sunset was awesome! Sweet potato tempura; who knew? And the special mushroom roll was pretty delicious. I was super skeptical because I couldn't imagine mushrooms in sushi, but it really worked.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  As for service, it was sloooooooow. Everyone's food came out at different times. My boyfriends mother ordered two appetizers as her entree but they didn't come until the very end, which was sort of odd. We waited a pretty long time for drinks to come to the table and even longer for them to get refilled. Also, the prices were excessive for what you received. Honestly. It didn't really make sense to me.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I'd probably return for the two special rolls, but that's it. Also, if you're big on innovative rolls, this place is not for you. They had about 6 on the entire menu.
                 </p>
                </div>

                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Went here for lunch and the sashimi was some of the best I've ever had. The owners were very friendly. The only complaint was from my boyfriend, who felt they were a bit heavy on the wasabi in some of the sushi he ordered.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I definitely plan on coming back here again! Prices incredibly reasonable too, with a massive list of lunch specials and really large portions.

                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Love it! Went there for dinner with some friends and enjoyed the authentic Japanese food. I was surprised that there was actually Japanese people serving and it seemed more authentic. The food was a bit pricey, like $6-10 for a sushi roll (6 pieces) but it was absolutely delicious. My boyfriend and friend ordered broiled chicken with white meat ($22) and it was great! My boyfriend kept talking about all night. :) it's great for once in a while becauae I live far and don't think I want to keep spending $8 per roll very often.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-28" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/28/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  We just moved to Carle Place and thus have been discovering the local eateries. We are big on sushi and have likened our favorites to Sushi of Gari, Sushi Yasuda, and Bar Masa. So we've had pretty good sushi.  I can honestly say the sushi here would rival those places.  It is very fresh. The owner buys everything fresh that day, if he doesn't like something for that day. Its not on the menu. The owners are a very sweet couple, and you can tell they want to please you and make you feel welcome. The fact that they have delicious food (that our 2 year old will eat) is a plus. Add to that the fact that they actually have one small section in the front, for kids to play with toys, and this is a plus all around! We will be regulars here for sure, and gladly so, as the trek to the city just got a heck of a long longer!
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-06-08" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   6/8/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  You can never imagine how amazing the Japanese food is unless you enter the home style Japanese restaurant. The host is a nice senior ages Japanese couple and you sometimes see their cute granddaughter! The food their is absolutely awesome. Since I've traveled to Japan several times. This place is the only place on Long Island. that reminds me of what I've eaten in Japan. Just don't know why ppl said its expensive their. You can't have cheap and healthy and fresh and delicious all the time. Please don't feel hesitate to have a try in this spot and you will be addicted to this small but warm place. Actually my friends and I are going to this restaurant at least once a week although we almost have tried everything they serve there. Still can't resist the desire to have some real authentic Japanese food there! Highly recommended.
                 </p>
                </div>

                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2012-05-16" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   5/16/2012
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  ...we are in Carle Place..and we need sushi... Yelp to the rescue as always!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We drove to the closest one and realized it was a buffet...I do not do Sushi buffets...just feels wrong. SO off we went to the next spot -- Koiso!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  This place doesn't look like much from the outside (and not really much from the inside)...it has such potential of being a cute place - just needs a little TLC. The whole time I was sitting there I wanted them to dim the lights and make it slightly more romantic feeling - less harsh lighting to hide some of the "rough edges" - so to speak.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The husband/wife combo are cute and make you feel right at home. Our food was very good - you must order the homemade gyoza! They pride themselves on it and I totally understand why! Delicious.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-09-09" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   9/9/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  3.4 stars. i'm now pretty convinced long islanders have no idea what quality japanese food tastes like. don't get me wrong, the food wasn't terrible, but it wasn't great either.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  the gyoza were solid. it tasted "homemade", which I don't necessarily say with endearment. i've had much better "homemade" gyozas in the city; the type of gyoza where you eat one and think to yourself, you wouldn't mind eating 50 more and calling it a meal. i ate 1 1/2 gyozas from koiso, said not bad, and wanted to move on.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  the roll i got was well put together, but it was dry, too salty, and bland.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  the fish tempura was just a gigantic misstep. the flesh of the fish was so dried out it was almost inedible.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  the chicken skewer was good, my broiled mackerel was well done, and the sashimi was fresh.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  overall the meal tasted very homemade in that it was good, but was clumsy and needed higher level recipes and tighter execution and technique to really elevate it from a homely kitchen to a legit restaurant.
                 </p>
                </div>
                <div class="review-footer clearfix">

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2012-07-19" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   7/19/2012
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   14 check-ins
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  True Mom and Pop place! The owner/ husband and wife team are very friendly and super sweet. They definitely dont rush you out of there but the down side is they arent always as attentive to fill up a water glass. It's walking distance from our house and only found it through Yelp. It's packed with locals so it's not surprising that the more you go the more you recognize the other locals.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  My boyfriend and I go here for sushi but the gyoza are home made and fresh and very yummy. While I don't eat seafood I'm a HUGE fan of the cucumber and avocado rolls but not a fan of seaweed so I opted for the soy bean paper as per the husband/sushi makers recommendation and I couldn't be happier! I know it's not "real sushi" but it's an amazing dish and very cheap. It comes with pickled ginger (spicy) which I lay on top before drinking it in some soy sauce.
                  <br/>
                  My boyfriend is much more of a real sushi person and his go to dishes are Alaskan, Fire cracker and Spicy Tuna... He said you can't go wrong!!
                 </p>
